# Text Elements
A truck driver slams on the brakes and the momentum of the truck changes from 
‹ 48000, 0, 0 › kg · m/s to ‹ 26000, 0, 0 › kg · m/s in 3.0 seconds due to a 
constant force of the road on the wheels of car. As a vector, write the net 
force exerted on the truck by the surroundings. ^CnY3wzTb

You were driving a car with velocity ‹ 20, 0, 10 › m/s. You quickly turned and 
braked, and your velocity became ‹ 15, 0, 13 › m/s. The mass of the car was 
1400 kg.

Find the change in momentum. ^gT6IyhHI

Find the impulse ^TNV1iOHp

Find the Net Force ^wAlOMBdc

A proton (mass 1.7 ✕ 10−27 kg) interacts electrically with a neutral HCl molecule located at the origin. At a certain time t, the proton's position is <1.6e-9, 0, 0>m and the proton's velocity is 

3300, 700, 0

 m/s.
 The force exerted on the proton by the HCl molecule is 

−1.12 ✕ 10−11, 0, 0

 N.
 At a time 
t + 4.2 ✕ 10−14 s,
 what is the approximate velocity of the proton? ^cwPC1P17
